<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="In_popular_culture">In popular culture</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Riverdale,_Bronx&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: In popular culture">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Riverdale has often been cited in literature, film and television.  Exteriors of many of Riverdale's locations have been used in both television and movie production.
</p><p><b>Literature</b>
</p>
<ul><li>In <i><a href="/wiki/On_the_Road" title="On the Road">On the Road</a></i>, <a href="/wiki/Horace_Mann_School" title="Horace Mann School">Horace Mann School</a>-educated <a href="/wiki/Jack_Kerouac" title="Jack Kerouac">Jack Kerouac</a> writes about getting off at a subway stop in Riverdale: "Filled with dreams of what I'd do in Chicago, in Denver, and then finally in San Fran, I took the Seventh Avenue Subway to the end of the line at 242nd Street, and there took a trolley into Yonkers; in downtown Yonkers I transferred to an outgoing trolley and went to the city limits on the east bank of the Hudson River."<sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tom_Wolfe" title="Tom Wolfe">Tom Wolfe</a>'s New York City-based 1987 novel <i><a href="/wiki/The_Bonfire_of_the_Vanities" title="The Bonfire of the Vanities">The Bonfire of the Vanities</a></i> includes many references to Riverdale.</li>
<li>In the 2003 novel <i><a href="/wiki/The_Devil_Wears_Prada_(novel)" title="The Devil Wears Prada (novel)">The Devil Wears Prada</a></i>, <a href="/wiki/Miranda_Priestly" class="mw-redirect" title="Miranda Priestly">Miranda Priestly</a>'s twin daughters attend the <a href="/wiki/Horace_Mann_School" title="Horace Mann School">Horace Mann School</a> in Riverdale.</li></ul>
<p><b>Films</b>
</p>
<ul><li>In 1938's <i><a href="/wiki/Bringing_Up_Baby" title="Bringing Up Baby">Bringing Up Baby</a></i>, <a href="/wiki/Katharine_Hepburn" title="Katharine Hepburn">Katharine Hepburn</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cary_Grant" title="Cary Grant">Cary Grant</a>'s characters visit a Riverdale estate owned by the fictional "Peabody" family.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Elia_Kazan" title="Elia Kazan">Elia Kazan</a>'s 1961 <i><a href="/wiki/Splendor_in_the_Grass" title="Splendor in the Grass">Splendor in the Grass</a></i> starring <a href="/wiki/Natalie_Wood" title="Natalie Wood">Natalie Wood</a> and <a href="/wiki/Warren_Beatty" title="Warren Beatty">Warren Beatty</a> included several high school scenes shot at <a href="/wiki/Horace_Mann_School" title="Horace Mann School">Horace Mann School</a>, such as a post-party scene outside Horace Mann's Prettyman Gymnasium.  The scenes at the asylum where Natalie Wood's character goes for treatment following her nervous breakdown were shot on one of the campuses of Riverdale Country School.</li>
<li>A mansion near <a href="/wiki/Wave_Hill" title="Wave Hill">Wave Hill</a> was used as a set in the film <i><a href="/wiki/The_Godfather" title="The Godfather">The Godfather</a></i> (1972).</li>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Martin_Scorsese" title="Martin Scorsese">Martin Scorsese</a>'s 1973 drama <i><a href="/wiki/Mean_Streets" title="Mean Streets">Mean Streets</a></i>, mobsters swindle a group of Riverdale teens trying to buy fireworks.</li>
<li>In the 1974 film <i><a href="/wiki/Crazy_Joe_(film)" title="Crazy Joe (film)">Crazy Joe</a></i>, an aerial shot follows characters driving from Manhattan, over the <a href="/wiki/Henry_Hudson_Bridge" title="Henry Hudson Bridge">Henry Hudson Bridge</a>, past buildings along the Hudson River, to <a href="/wiki/Wave_Hill" title="Wave Hill">Wave Hill</a>, where an outdoor scene continues.</li>
<li>Much of <a href="/wiki/Woody_Allen" title="Woody Allen">Woody Allen</a>'s film <i><a href="/wiki/Husbands_and_Wives" title="Husbands and Wives">Husbands and Wives</a></i> (1992) takes place at the Riverdale residence of characters Jack and Sally.</li>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Spike_Lee" title="Spike Lee">Spike Lee</a>'s 2002 film <i><a href="/wiki/25th_Hour" title="25th Hour">25th Hour</a></i>, <a href="/wiki/Rosario_Dawson" title="Rosario Dawson">Rosario Dawson</a>'s character Naturelle snaps at <a href="/wiki/Edward_Norton" title="Edward Norton">Edward Norton</a>'s character Monty, "What, I can't be from Riverdale?"</li>
<li>In the 2004 film <i><a href="/wiki/Secret_Window" title="Secret Window">Secret Window</a></i>  Mort Rainey's ex-wife lives in Riverdale, New York; several camera shots show the <a href="/wiki/Henry_Hudson_Parkway" title="Henry Hudson Parkway">Henry Hudson Parkway</a> and glimpses of Riverdale.</li>
<li>In the 2005 biopic <i><a href="/wiki/Good_Night,_and_Good_Luck" title="Good Night, and Good Luck">Good Night, and Good Luck</a></i>, <a href="/wiki/George_Clooney" title="George Clooney">George Clooney</a>'s character <a href="/wiki/Fred_W._Friendly" title="Fred W. Friendly">Fred W. Friendly</a> states that he and his family are relocating to a "nice house in Riverdale".</li>
<li>In the 2010 romantic drama <i><a href="/wiki/Blue_Valentine_(film)" title="Blue Valentine (film)">Blue Valentine</a></i>, <a href="/wiki/Michelle_Williams_(actress)" title="Michelle Williams (actress)">Michelle Williams</a>'s character is encouraged to work in Riverdale.</li>
<li>In the <a href="/wiki/The_Secret_Life_of_Walter_Mitty_(2013_film)" title="The Secret Life of Walter Mitty (2013 film)">2013 remake</a> of the film <i><a href="/wiki/The_Secret_Life_of_Walter_Mitty_(1947_film)" title="The Secret Life of Walter Mitty (1947 film)">The Secret Life of Walter Mitty</a></i>, Windsor South, an apartment building along the <a href="/wiki/Henry_Hudson_Parkway" title="Henry Hudson Parkway">Henry Hudson Parkway</a>, is shown.<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<p><b>Television</b>
</p>
<ul><li>On television's <i><a href="/wiki/Mad_Men" title="Mad Men">Mad Men</a></i>, <a href="/wiki/Joan_Holloway" title="Joan Holloway">Joan Holloway</a> reveals that she and her husband are considering relocating to Riverdale, explaining, "It's close to Columbia Presbyterian. Plus, Greg wants a yard".<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>In Season 3, Episode 2 of <i><a href="/wiki/Gossip_Girl" title="Gossip Girl">Gossip Girl</a></i>, <a href="/wiki/Blair_Waldorf" title="Blair Waldorf">Blair Waldorf</a> says, "Riverdale doesn't count".</li>
<li>In Season 3, Episode 19 of <i><a href="/wiki/Wizards_of_Waverly_Place" title="Wizards of Waverly Place">Wizards of Waverly Place</a></i>, Theresa Russo (<a href="/wiki/Maria_Canals_Barrera" class="mw-redirect" title="Maria Canals Barrera">Maria Canals Barrera</a>) assumes that Nancy Lukey (<a href="/wiki/Bella_Thorne" title="Bella Thorne">Bella Thorne</a>), her son's newly introduced girlfriend, is a rich kid because she lives in Riverdale.</li></ul>
